#Made by Lord Bogdanoff
focus_tree = {
	id = belorussia_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = BLR
		}
	}

	# Sets Camera to Opening of the Political Tree
	initial_show_position = { x = 78 y = 1 }
	#Economic branch
	focus = {
		id = BLR_Economic
		icon = blr_our_ruble
		x = 93
		y = 0
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
		cost = 5
		ai_will_do = { factor = 155 }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_Economic"
			increase_economic_growth = yes
			calculate_interest_rate = yes
		}
	}
	#Beginning of reforms Belarusian Railway
	focus = {
		id = BLR_reforms_Belarusian_Railway

		cost = 1
		relative_position_id = BLR_Economic

		}
	}
	#Construction of a new railway station in Minsk
	focus = {

		cost = 5
		relative_position_id = BLR_Economic

				limit = { emerging_reactionaries_are_in_power = yes }

	#Duying vilages
	focus = {
		id = BLR_Problem_duying_vilages
		icon = house
		x = 0
		y = 3
		cost = 7
		ai_will_do = { factor = 155 }
		relative_position_id = BLR_Economic
		available = {
			has_idea = BLR_villages
		}
		prerequisite = { focus = BLR_Belshina }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_Problem_duying_vilages"
			custom_effect_tooltip = BLR_villages_TT
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = communism
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					has_idea = BLR_villages
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BLR_villages
					add_idea = BLR_villages_other
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
					has_idea = BLR_villages
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BLR_villages
					add_idea = BLR_villages_west
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = nationalist
					has_idea = BLR_villages
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BLR_villages
					add_idea = BLR_villages_nati
				}
			}
		}
	}

	##Nationalists
	focus = {
		id = BLR_Pazniak
		icon = blr_choose
		x = 104
		y = 7
		available = {
			OR = {
				nationalist_right_wing_populists_are_in_power = yes
				nationalist_monarchists_are_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 155
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_global_flag = BLR_NATIONALIST_PATH
			}
		}
		cost = 1
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_Pazniak"
			add_political_power = 100
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = CSTO_member }
					leave_faction = yes
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.25
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = BLR_kal_with
						OR = {
							nationalist_right_wing_populists_are_in_power = yes
							nationalist_monarchists_are_in_power = yes
						}
					}
					SOV = { remove_ideas = SOV_kal_with }
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = BLR_kal_with
						add_idea = BLR_kal_without
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}
